#New regex 1: PPOSWRES->MRES  e.g -650A>T; instad of > an arrow is also permitted, see(PMID: 19568425) 
(?:^|[\s\(\[\'"/,;])(?P<pos>(-{0,1})[1-9][0-9]*(?:\s?[+-]\s?[1-9][0-9]*)?)\s{0,1}(?P<wt_res>[ATGC])\s{0,1}(?:-{0,2}>|â†’)\s{0,1}(?P<mut_res>[ATGC])(?=([.,\s)\]\'":;\-?!/]|$))[CASE_SENSITIVE]
